                function revslider_showDoubleJqueryError(sliderID) {
                    var errorMessage = "Revolution Slider Error: You have some jquery.js library include that comes after the revolution files js include.";

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){

        $("select[name='car_brand_id']").on("change", function(){
            var brand_id = $(this).val();
            var token = $("input[name='_token']").val();
            $.ajax({
                url: "~/ar/ajax/models",
                method: 'POST',
                data: {brand_id:brand_id, _token:token},
                success: function(data) {
                $("select[name='car_model_id'").html('');
                $("select[name='car_model_id'").html(data.options);
                }
            });
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){

        $("select[name='car_model_id']").on("change", function(){
            var model_id = $(this).val();
            var token = $("input[name='_token']").val();
            $.ajax({
                url: "~/ar/ajax/model_types",
                method: 'POST',
                data: {model_id:model_id, _token:token},
                success: function(data) {
                $("select[name='car_model_type'").html('');
                $("select[name='car_model_type'").html(data.options);
                }
            });
        });
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){

        

        $("#search-box").keypress(function(){
            var  search_text = $(this).val();
            var token = $("input[name='_token']").val();
            console.log(search_text);
            

            $.ajax({
                url: "~/ar/search_ajax",
                method: 'POST',
                data: {search_text:search_text, _token:token},
                success: function(data) {
                    console.log(data);
                    $(".results").slideDown();
                    $(".results").html('');
                    $(".results").html(data);

                }
            });
            
        });
    });
</script>

      <script>
  
      $(document).mouseup(function(e) 
      {
          var container = $("#form_call");
  
          var search_results = $(".results");
  
          var result_mobile = $(".resultsm");
  
          var social_share =  $("#social_btns_wraper");
  
          var searchOnFixed = $("#searchOnFixed");
  
          // if the target of the click isn't the container nor a descendant of the container
          if (!container.is(e.target) && container.has(e.target).length === 0) 
          {
              container.slideUp();
          }
  
          if (!search_results.is(e.target) && search_results.has(e.target).length === 0) 
          {
              search_results.slideUp();
          }
  
          if (!result_mobile.is(e.target) && result_mobile.has(e.target).length === 0) 
          {
              result_mobile.slideUp();
          }
  
          if (!social_share.is(e.target) && social_share.has(e.target).length === 0) 
          {
              social_share.slideUp();
          }
  
          if (!searchOnFixed.is(e.target) && searchOnFixed.has(e.target).length === 0) 
          {
              searchOnFixed.slideUp();
          }
  
  
      });
  
  
      $(document).ready(function(){
  
          $("#closeSearchMobile").click(function(e){
              e.preventDefault();
              $(".resultsm").slideUp();
          });
  
          $('.addToFavLink').tooltip();
  
  
          //$('.ttt').lightBox();
          // Display form get mobile before call Or whats
          $(".displayPopup").on("click", function(e){
              e.preventDefault();
              $(this).addClass('hoverd').siblings().removeClass('hoverd');
              
              if($(this).data('type') == "phone"){
                  $("#form_call").slideDown();
                  $('#form_call').find('button i').removeClass('fa-whatsapp').removeClass('fab').addClass('fas').addClass('fa-phone');
                  $("#phonenumber_type").val("1");
              }
              else if($(this).data('type') == "whats"){
                  $("#form_call").slideDown();
                  //$(this).find('button i').removeClass('fas fa-phone').addClass('fab fa-whatsapp');
                  $('#form_call').find('button i').removeClass('fa-phone').removeClass('fas').addClass('fab').addClass('fa-whatsapp');
                  $("#phonenumber_type").val("2");
              }
              else if($(this).data('type') == "share"){
                  $("#social_btns_wraper").slideDown();
              }
              else if($(this).data('type') == "search"){
                  $("#searchOnFixed").slideDown();
              }
          });
          
          // Why Saleh Carusal Used in:
          // Home

          // Advanced Search Button Open #advancedSearchModal Modal
          $('#advancedSearch').on("click", function(e){
              e.preventDefault();

              $("#searchMobile").slideUp();

          /* Toggle Mobile Menu */
          $("#topIcon").on("click", function () {
              if ($("#myTopnav").hasClass("responsive")) {
                  $("#myTopnav").slideUp();
                  $("#myTopnav").removeClass("responsive");
                  $("#topIcon").removeClass("responsive");
                  //console.log('opend nav');
              } else {
                  $("#myTopnav").slideDown().addClass("responsive");
                  $("#topIcon").addClass("responsive");
                  //console.log('closed nav');
              }
          });
          /* Toggle Search Mobile */
          $("#searchIcon").on("click", function () {
              if ($(".header").hasClass("hasSearch")) {
                  $("#searchMobile").slideUp();
                  $(".header").removeClass("hasSearch");
                  $(".header").removeClass("hasSearch");
                  //console.log('opend nav');
              } else {
                  $("#searchMobile").slideDown().addClass("hasSearch");
                  $(".header").addClass("hasSearch");
                  //console.log('closed nav');
              }
          });

      /* Fixed Header in top */ 
  
  
       // if is mobile Fixed purchace tab on bottom
      // else if is Desktop Fixed purchace tab on Top
      var isMobile = window.matchMedia("only screen and (max-width: 760px)").matches;
  
      if (isMobile) {
          
          function fixDiv() {
              var $cache = $('#getFixed');
              if ($(window).scrollTop() > 300){
                  $cache.slideDown();
                  document.getElementById('getFixed').style.display = "block";
                  $cache.css({
                      'position': 'fixed',
                      'bottom': '0',
                      'top': 'auto',
                      'display':'block'
                  });
                  $('#footer').css({
                      'margin-bottom':'50px',
                  });
                  $('#callOnFixed').hide();
              }else{
                  $cache.slideUp();
                  document.getElementById('getFixed').style.display = "none";
                  $cache.css({
                      'position': 'relative',
                      'bottom': 'auto',
                      'display':'none',
                  });
                  $('#footer').css({
                      'margin-bottom':'0',
                  });
              }
          }
          $(window).scroll(fixDiv);
          fixDiv();
  
      }else{
  
          function fixDiv() {
              var $cache = $('#getFixed');
              if ($(window).scrollTop() > 300){
                  $cache.slideDown('fast');
                  $cache.css({
                      'position': 'fixed',
                      'top': '0',
                      'display':'block'
                  });
              }else{
                  $cache.slideUp();
                  $cache.css({
                      'position': 'relative',
                      'top': 'auto',
                      'display':'none'
                  });
              }
          }
          $(window).scroll(fixDiv);
          fixDiv();
      }
  
      </script>
  
  <script type="text/javascript">
      $(document).ready(function(){
  
          
  
          $("#toHeadSearch").keypress(function(){
              var  search_text = $(this).val();
              var token = $("input[name='_token']").val();
              console.log(search_text);
              
  
              $.ajax({
                  url: "~/ar/search_ajax",
                  method: 'POST',
                  data: {search_text:search_text, _token:token},
                  success: function(data) {
                      $(".resultsm").slideDown();
                      $(".resultsm").html('');
                      $(".resultsm").html(data);
  
                  }
              });
              
          });
  
          $("#toHeadSearch2").keypress(function(){
              var  search_text = $(this).val();
              var token = $("input[name='_token']").val();
              console.log(search_text);
              
  
              $.ajax({
                  url: "~/ar/search_ajax",
                  method: 'POST',
                  data: {search_text:search_text, _token:token},
                  success: function(data) {
                      $(".resultsm").slideDown();
                      $(".resultsm").html('');
                      $(".resultsm").html(data);
  
                  }
              });
              
          });
      });
  </script>
  
  
  
  
  
  <script type="text/javascript">
      $(document).ready(function(){
  
          $("select[name='mcar_brand_id']").on("change", function(){
              var brand_id = $(this).val();
              var token = $("input[name='_token']").val();
              $.ajax({
                  url: "~/ar/ajax/models",
                  method: 'POST',
                  data: {brand_id:brand_id, _token:token},
                  success: function(data) {
                  $("select[name='mcar_model_id'").html('');
                  $("select[name='mcar_model_id'").html(data.options);
                  }
              });
          });
      });
  </script>
  
  <script type="text/javascript">

  <script type="text/javascript">
  
  


            let openCall = "~/web/img/ArCall.svg";
    
    let endCall = "~/web/img/ArEnd.svg";
    let x = document.getElementById("web_stdy");
    var btnz = x.shadowRoot;

    btnz.addEventListener("click", changeIcon, true);
  
    $(btnz).find('.call-us-toolbar').find('.button_3Mr5m').find('svg').replaceWith('<img src="'+openCall+'" width="52">');
      
    $(btnz).find('.user-container-phone-only_3VdZn').find('.button-end-call_1ZlXf').find('svg').replaceWith('<img src="'+openCall+'" width="52">');
    window.onload = function(){
        $(btnz).find('.call-us-toolbar').find('.button_3Mr5m').find('svg').replaceWith('<img src="'+openCall+'" width="52">');
        $(btnz).find('.call-us-toolbar').find('.button-end-call_1ZlXf').find('svg').replaceWith('<img src="'+endCall+'" width="52">');
    };

    function changeIcon()
    {
        $(btnz).find('.call-us-toolbar').find('.button_3Mr5m').find('svg').replaceWith('<img src="'+openCall+'" width="52">');
        $(btnz).find('.user-container-phone-only_3VdZn').find('.button-end-call_1ZlXf').find('svg').replaceWith('<img src="'+endCall+'" width="52">');
        console.log('changeIcon');
    }
      
    var sheet = new CSSStyleSheet
    sheet.replaceSync( `.root_2kd-q .call-us-toolbar button { background-color: transparent }`)
    x.shadowRoot.adoptedStyleSheets = [ sheet ] 
  </script>
